# Hindsight ŌĆö Implementation Plan

## Context

Hindsight (`hindsight-journal`) is a journaling retrospection and analytics plugin for Obsidian. Inspired by ObJournal but significantly more capable ŌĆö it reads existing daily notes with dynamic frontmatter fields, indexes them, and provides calendar views, charts, echoes (look-back), pulse (stats), threads (tags/topics), and more via React within Obsidian ItemView shells.

This is a personal-use project built at a relaxed pace. No MVP rush ŌĆö features ship when they're ready. Must comply with Obsidian community plugin guidelines throughout (`.agent/rules/obsidian-plugin-guidelines.md`).

---

## Decisions Locked In

| Decision | Choice |
|----------|--------|
| Plugin ID | `hindsight-journal` |
| State management | Zustand |
| Charting | Chart.js (~200KB) for time-series line charts, bar charts, scatter plots; React SVG for heatmaps/grids/sparklines. |
| Thumbnails | IndexedDB cache with LRU eviction |
| Folder scanning | Recursive (mixed folder structures) |
| Frontmatter fields | Dynamically detected, not hardcoded |
| Note creation | Read-only first, note creation added later |
| CSS | Manual BEM prefixing (`hindsight-*`), PostCSS for `@import` only, CSS variables for theming |
| Date source of truth | Frontmatter `date` field is authoritative; filename regex is candidate filter only |
| Mobile | `isDesktopOnly: false`, 44px touch targets, tap alternatives for hover |
| Testing | Vitest with jsdom, X.5 phase after each feature phase, output piped to `test-output.txt` |

---

## Journal Data Structure (Brad's Vault)

**Folder:** `Health/Mental Health/Tracker Notes` (configurable)
**Structure:** Mixed ŌĆö some months in subfolders (`2026/January/`), some flat in root. Must scan recursively.
**Filename pattern:** `YYYY-MM-DD, Day.md` (e.g., `2026-03-05, Thursday.md`)

**Frontmatter fields (dynamic ŌĆö plugin detects these, does NOT hardcode them):**
```yaml
created: "05:35am, 2026-03-05"
morning_meds_taken:      # boolean
light_therapy:           # number (minutes)
sleep_duration:          # number (hours)
weight:                  # number (lbs)
workout:                 # boolean
crohns_status:           # string
daydreaming_pull:        # number
anxiety:                 # number
mood:                    # number (1-10)
energy:                  # number (1-10)
evening_meds_taken:      # boolean
tags:                    # string[]
date: "2026-03-05"       # string (ISO date)
studying_hours_done:     # number
```

**Note sections (## headings):** Dreams, The Must Dos, High Priority Tasks, Scratchpad / Quick Capture, What Actually Happened, Notes / Thoughts, Meds, Daily Check-in, Tomorrow's Top 3, Social Check-In, Switchboard Log, Quest Board Activity

---

---

## Testing Approach

Each feature phase (1-10) is followed by an X.5 testing phase. Testing phases are a **SEPARATE task** ŌĆö never started until Brad has manually confirmed the parent phase works in Obsidian.

**Test runner workflow** (per `.agent/workflows/test.md`):
```powershell
npx vitest run 2>&1 | Out-File -Encoding utf8 test-output.txt
Get-Content test-output.txt -Tail 20
```

**What to test per layer:**
- **Utils:** Unit tests for all pure functions (no mocks needed)
- **Services:** Unit tests with mocked Obsidian API. Test parsing, field detection, metric computation, date math.
- **Stores:** Unit tests for Zustand actions and selectors. Verify state transitions.
- **Integration:** Cross-service tests where services compose together.

**What NOT to test (manual only):**
- React components (visual testing in Obsidian)
- Obsidian view lifecycle (mount/unmount)
- Visual rendering

**Mock strategy:** `test/mocks/obsidian.ts` aliased via `vitest.config.ts` resolve ŌĆö same pattern as Quest Board. Stubs `TFile`, `TFolder`, `Vault`, `MetadataCache`, `normalizePath`, `App`, `Plugin`, `Setting`, `PluginSettingTab`, `ItemView`, `WorkspaceLeaf`, `Notice`, `Menu`, `requestUrl`.

---

## Reference Patterns (from Quest Board)

**These files in Quest Board should be used as templates. Copy and adapt, don't reinvent:**

| Pattern | Quest Board Reference | Adapt For |
|---------|----------------------|-----------|
| esbuild config | `esbuild.config.mjs` | Copy verbatim |
| Deploy script | `deploy.mjs` | Change `quest-board` ŌåÆ `hindsight-journal`, remove asset folder logic |
| tsconfig | `tsconfig.json` | Copy verbatim |
| PostCSS config | `postcss.config.cjs` | Copy verbatim |
| Vitest config | `vitest.config.ts` | Copy, update paths |
| Obsidian mock | `test/mocks/obsidian.ts` | Copy, add `MetadataCache` mock |
| ItemView shell | `src/views/QuestBoardView.tsx` | Template for both views |
| manifest.json | `manifest.json` | New ID, name, description |
| package.json scripts | `package.json` scripts section | Same pattern, remove manifest:generate |

**ItemView React mounting pattern (non-negotiable):**
```typescript
async onOpen(): Promise<void> {
    const container = this.containerEl.children[1];
    container.empty();
    container.addClass('hindsight-container');
    this.root = createRoot(container as HTMLElement);
    this.root.render(<Component plugin={this.plugin} app={this.app} />);
}

async onClose(): Promise<void> {
    if (this.root) {
        this.root.unmount();
        this.root = null;
    }
}
```

---

# DETAILED PHASES (0-4)

---

## Phase 0: Project Scaffold (~1 session)

**Goal:** Bootable plugin that loads in Obsidian, shows in settings, has the full build pipeline working, vitest runs (even with 0 tests). Everything after this starts from a working baseline.

### Files to Create

**`package.json`**
```json
{
    "name": "hindsight-journal",
    "version": "0.1.0",
    "description": "Visualize and reflect on your journal entries.",
    "main": "main.js",
    "scripts": {
        "css:build": "postcss src/styles/index.css -o styles.css",
        "css:watch": "postcss src/styles/index.css -o styles.css --watch",
        "dev": "node esbuild.config.mjs",
        "build": "npm run css:build && tsc -noEmit -skipLibCheck && node esbuild.config.mjs production",
        "deploy:test": "npm run build && node deploy.mjs test",
        "deploy:staging": "npm run build && node deploy.mjs staging",
        "deploy:production": "npm run build && node deploy.mjs production",
        "test": "vitest",
        "test:run": "vitest run"
    },
    "dependencies": {
        "react": "^18.2.0",
        "react-dom": "^18.2.0",
        "zustand": "^4.4.0"
    },
    "devDependencies": {
        "@types/node": "^20.10.0",
        "@types/react": "^18.2.0",
        "@types/react-dom": "^18.2.0",
        "builtin-modules": "^3.3.0",
        "esbuild": "^0.19.0",
        "jsdom": "^28.1.0",
        "obsidian": "latest",
        "postcss": "^8.5.6",
        "postcss-cli": "^11.0.1",
        "postcss-import": "^16.1.1",
        "tslib": "^2.6.0",
        "typescript": "^5.3.0",
        "vitest": "^4.0.18"
    }
}
```
Note: Chart.js is NOT added yet ŌĆö it arrives in Phase 5. Keep deps minimal until needed.

**`manifest.json`**
```json
{
    "id": "hindsight-journal",
    "name": "Hindsight Journal",
    "version": "0.1.0",
    "minAppVersion": "1.6.5",
    "description": "Visualize and reflect on your journal entries with calendars, charts, and retrospective insights.",
    "author": "Brad Wales",
    "authorUrl": "https://github.com/thuban87",
    "isDesktopOnly": false
}
```

**`versions.json`**
```json
{ "0.1.0": "1.6.5" }
```

> **Note:** `minAppVersion` set to `1.6.5` because `getFolderByPath()` was introduced in Obsidian 1.6.5. Using a lower version would cause runtime errors for users on 1.6.0ŌĆō1.6.4.

**`esbuild.config.mjs`** ŌĆö Copy verbatim from Quest Board (same externals, same banner, same CJS format).

**`tsconfig.json`** ŌĆö Copy verbatim from Quest Board (strict, jsx: react-jsx, path alias `@/*` ŌåÆ `src/*`).

**`postcss.config.cjs`** ŌĆö Copy verbatim from Quest Board (`require('postcss-import')`).

**`deploy.mjs`** ŌĆö Adapted from Quest Board:
- Change `VAULTS` paths: `quest-board` ŌåÆ `hindsight-journal` in all three environments
- Remove `ASSET_FOLDERS` entirely (Hindsight has no asset files to deploy)
- Remove the asset-copying logic from the `deploy()` function
- Keep the production confirmation prompt

**`vitest.config.ts`** ŌĆö Adapted from Quest Board:
```typescript
import { defineConfig } from 'vitest/config';
import path from 'path';

export default defineConfig({
    resolve: {
        alias: {
            'obsidian': path.resolve(__dirname, 'test/mocks/obsidian.ts'),
        },
    },
    test: {
        environment: 'jsdom',
        setupFiles: ['./test/setup.ts'],
        include: ['test/**/*.test.ts'],
        exclude: ['node_modules/**'],
        globals: true,
    },
});
```

**`test/setup.ts`** ŌĆö Empty for now, placeholder:
```typescript
// Vitest setup file ŌĆö add global test configuration here as needed
```

**`test/mocks/obsidian.ts`** ŌĆö Copy from Quest Board's `test/mocks/obsidian.ts`, then add:
```typescript
// Add MetadataCache mock (not in Quest Board's mock)
export class MetadataCache {
    getFileCache(_file: TFile): { frontmatter?: Record<string, unknown> } | null {
        return null;
    }
    on(_event: string, _callback: (...args: unknown[]) => void): void { }
}
```
Also update `App` class to include `metadataCache`:
```typescript
export class App {
    vault = new Vault();
    metadataCache = new MetadataCache();
    workspace = {
        onLayoutReady: (cb: () => void) => cb(),
        getLeavesOfType: (_type: string) => [],
        getLeftLeaf: (_split: boolean) => null,
        getLeaf: (_type: string) => null,
        openLinkText: async (_link: string, _source: string) => {},
    };
    fileManager = {
        processFrontMatter: async (_file: TFile, _fn: (fm: Record<string, unknown>) => void) => {},
    };
}
```

**`main.ts`** ŌĆö Thin orchestrator:
```typescript
import { Plugin } from 'obsidian';
import { HindsightSettingTab } from './src/settings';
import { DEFAULT_SETTINGS, HindsightSettings } from './src/types';

export default class HindsightPlugin extends Plugin {
    settings: HindsightSettings = DEFAULT_SETTINGS;

    async onload(): Promise<void> {
        await this.loadSettings();
        this.addSettingTab(new HindsightSettingTab(this.app, this));

        // Services and views will be registered here in later phases
        console.debug('Hindsight Journal loaded');
    }

    onunload(): void {
        // Cleanup will be added as services/views are registered
    }

    async loadSettings(): Promise<void> {
        this.settings = Object.assign({}, DEFAULT_SETTINGS, await this.loadData());
    }

    async saveSettings(): Promise<void> {
        await this.saveData(this.settings);
    }
}
```

**`src/types.ts`** ŌĆö Core interfaces:
```typescript
/** Plugin settings */
export interface HindsightSettings {
    /** Path to the journal folder (scanned recursively) */
    journalFolder: string;
    /** Path to weekly review folder (optional) */
    weeklyReviewFolder: string;
    /** Whether to on plugin load */
    enableSidebar: boolean;
    /** Whether to generate and cache image thumbnails */
    thumbnailsEnabled: boolean;
    /** Whether to show the morning briefing panel in the sidebar */
    morningBriefingEnabled: boolean;
    /** Sections whose checkboxes count toward productivity score (whitelist) */
    productivitySections: string[];
    /** Sections whose checkboxes are excluded from productivity score (blacklist) */
    excludedSections: string[];
}

export const DEFAULT_SETTINGS: HindsightSettings = {
    journalFolder: 'Journal',
    weeklyReviewFolder: '',
    enableSidebar: true,
    thumbnailsEnabled: false,
    morningBriefingEnabled: false,
    productivitySections: [],
    excludedSections: ['Meds'],
};

/**
 * A single parsed journal entry.
 *
 * ARCHITECTURE NOTE: rawContent is NOT stored here to avoid holding
 * the full text of every journal entry in memory. With 700+ entries,
 * that would be 3-4MB of heap. Instead:
 * - Frontmatter is extracted via metadataCache (zero I/O)
 * - Sections, word count, and image paths are computed during
 *   background indexing (Phase 1 pass 2) and cached here
 * - Full text is lazy-loaded via vault.cachedRead() on demand
 *   (e.g., for full-text search in the Lens feature)
 */
export interface JournalEntry {
    /** Vault-relative file path */
    filePath: string;
    /** Parsed date ŌĆö sourced from frontmatter `date` field (authoritative), filename as fallback */
    date: Date;
    /** Day of week (e.g., "Thursday") */
    dayOfWeek: string;
    /** All frontmatter key-value pairs (dynamic) */
    frontmatter: Record<string, unknown>;
    /** Parsed sections by heading name (populated during background pass 2) */
    sections: Record<string, string>;
    /** Word count (computed during pass 2, 0 until then) */
    wordCount: number;
    /** Vault-relative paths to embedded images (populated during pass 2) */
    imagePaths: string[];
    /** File modification timestamp (ms) */
    mtime: number;
    /** Whether pass 2 (full content parsing) has completed for this entry */
    fullyIndexed: boolean;
    /** Entry quality score (0-100): percentage of detected fields that are filled */
    qualityScore: number;
}

/** Describes a detected frontmatter field across all entries */
export interface FrontmatterField {
    /** Field key as it appears in frontmatter */
    key: string;
    /** Inferred type */
    type: 'number' | 'boolean' | 'string' | 'date' | 'string[]';
    /** How many entries have a non-empty value for this field */
    coverage: number;
    /** Total entries scanned */
    total: number;
    /** Min/max for numeric fields */
    range?: { min: number; max: number };
}

/** A single data point for charting */
export interface MetricDataPoint {
    /** Unix timestamp in milliseconds */
    date: number;
    /** Value, or null if missing */
    value: number | null;
}

/** A time range for queries */
export interface DateRange {
    start: Date;
    end: Date;
}

/** Parsed section from a journal entry */
export interface ParsedSection {
    /** Heading text (without the ## prefix) */
    heading: string;
    /** Heading level (1-6) */
    level: number;
    /** Raw markdown content under the heading */
    content: string;
}
```

**`src/settings.ts`** ŌĆö Settings tab:
```typescript
import { PluginSettingTab, App, Setting } from 'obsidian';
import type HindsightPlugin from '../main';

export class HindsightSettingTab extends PluginSettingTab {
    plugin: HindsightPlugin;

    constructor(app: App, plugin: HindsightPlugin) {
        super(app, plugin);
        this.plugin = plugin;
    }

    display(): void {
        const { containerEl } = this;
        containerEl.empty();

        new Setting(containerEl)
            .setHeading()
            .setName('Journal');

        // IMPORTANT: Text inputs use onBlur (not onChange) to avoid
        // hammering saveSettings() on every keystroke.
        // onChange would trigger disk I/O per character typed.
        new Setting(containerEl)
            .setName('Journal folder')
            .setDesc('Folder containing your daily notes (scanned recursively).')
            .addText(text => {
                text.setPlaceholder('e.g., Journal')
                    .setValue(this.plugin.settings.journalFolder);
                text.inputEl.addEventListener('blur', async () => {
                    const newFolder = text.inputEl.value.trim();
                    if (newFolder !== this.plugin.settings.journalFolder) {
                        this.plugin.settings.journalFolder = newFolder;
                        await this.plugin.saveSettings();
                        // Trigger re-index with the new folder
                        this.plugin.journalIndex?.reconfigure(newFolder);
                    }
                });
            });

        new Setting(containerEl)
            .setName('Weekly review folder')
            .setDesc('Folder containing weekly review notes (optional).')
            .addText(text => {
                text.setPlaceholder('e.g., Weekly Reviews')
                    .setValue(this.plugin.settings.weeklyReviewFolder);
                text.inputEl.addEventListener('blur', async () => {
                    const value = text.inputEl.value.trim();
                    if (value !== this.plugin.settings.weeklyReviewFolder) {
                        this.plugin.settings.weeklyReviewFolder = value;
                        await this.plugin.saveSettings();
                    }
                });
            });

        new Setting(containerEl)
            .setHeading()
            .setName('Appearance');

        new Setting(containerEl)
            .setName('Open sidebar on startup')
            .setDesc('Automatically open the Hindsight sidebar when the plugin loads.')
            .addToggle(toggle => toggle
                .setValue(this.plugin.settings.enableSidebar)
                .onChange(async (value) => {
                    this.plugin.settings.enableSidebar = value;
                    await this.plugin.saveSettings();
                }));
    }
}
```

## Phase 1: Journal Index Service + Store (~1-2 sessions) Ō£ģ COMPLETE

**Goal:** Recursively scan the journal folder, parse every daily note (filename ŌåÆ date, frontmatter, sections, images, word count), store them in a Zustand store, and keep the index alive with file event watching. This is the data backbone everything else depends on.

### Files to Create

**`src/utils/fileNameParser.ts`** (~40 lines)

Parses filenames matching the pattern `YYYY-MM-DD, Day.md`:
```typescript
export interface ParsedFileName {
    date: Date;
    dayOfWeek: string;
}

/**
 * Parse a journal filename into date and day of week.
 * Expected format: "2026-03-05, Thursday.md"
 * Returns null if the filename doesn't match the expected pattern.
 */
export function parseJournalFileName(filename: string): ParsedFileName | null {
    // Regex: YYYY-MM-DD, DayName.md
    const match = filename.match(/^(\d{4})-(\d{2})-(\d{2}),\s+(\w+)\.md$/);
    if (!match) return null;

    const [, year, month, day, dayOfWeek] = match;
    const date = new Date(Number(year), Number(month) - 1, Number(day));

    // Validate the date is real (catches things like Feb 31)
    if (isNaN(date.getTime())) return null;
    if (date.getFullYear() !== Number(year)) return null;
    if (date.getMonth() !== Number(month) - 1) return null;
    if (date.getDate() !== Number(day)) return null;

    return { date, dayOfWeek };
}
```

**`src/utils/dateUtils.ts`** (~80 lines)

Date comparison and range utilities. All functions use native `Date` ŌĆö NO moment.js:
```typescript
/** Check if two dates are the same calendar day */
export function isSameDay(a: Date, b: Date): boolean

/** Check if two dates are in the same ISO week */
export function isSameWeek(a: Date, b: Date): boolean

/** Get ISO week number for a date */
export function getISOWeek(date: Date): number

/** Get all dates in a range (inclusive) */
export function getDatesInRange(start: Date, end: Date): Date[]

/** Format date as YYYY-MM-DD string */
export function formatDateISO(date: Date): string

/** Get start of day (midnight) for a date */
export function startOfDay(date: Date): Date

/** Get the number of days between two dates */
export function daysBetween(a: Date, b: Date): number

/** Check if a date falls within a range (inclusive) */
export function isInRange(date: Date, range: DateRange): boolean
```

**`src/services/SectionParserService.ts`** (~120 lines)

Pure functions ŌĆö no Obsidian API dependency, fully testable:
```typescript
/**
 * Parse markdown content into sections keyed by heading text.
 * Processes ## (h2) headings as top-level sections.
 * ### (h3) headings are included in their parent ## section's content.
 * Headings inside code blocks (``` ... ```) are ignored.
 */
export function parseSections(content: string): Record<string, string>

/**
 * Extract a single section by heading name.
 * Returns null if the heading doesn't exist.
 */
export function extractSection(content: string, heading: string): string | null

/**
 * Extract all image embed paths from markdown content.
 * Handles both ![[image.png]] (wikilink) and ![alt](path.png) (standard) syntax.
 * Returns vault-relative paths.
 */
export function extractImagePaths(content: string): string[]

/**
 * Count words in text content (strips markdown syntax first).
 */
export function countWords(text: string): number

/**
 * Strip markdown syntax AND HTML tags to produce clean plain text.
 * Removes: [[links]], [text](urls), **bold**, *italic*, # headings,
 * - [ ] checkboxes, > blockquotes, ``` code blocks ```,
 * and all HTML tags (<script>, <img>, <div>, etc.).
 * HTML stripping is defense-in-depth ŌĆö Obsidian notes can contain raw HTML,
 * and while React JSX escapes by default, stripping here ensures
 * excerpts are always safe plain text regardless of rendering context.
 */
export function stripMarkdown(text: string): string
```

**`src/services/FrontmatterService.ts`** (~130 lines)

Analyzes frontmatter across entries to detect fields dynamically:
```typescript
/**
 * Scan all entries and detect what frontmatter fields exist,
 * their types, coverage (how many entries have them), and ranges.
 */
export function detectFields(entries: JournalEntry[]): FrontmatterField[]

/**
 * Infer the type of a frontmatter field from its values across entries.
 * Rules: if all non-null values are numbers ŌåÆ 'number',
 *        if all are true/false ŌåÆ 'boolean',
 *        if all are arrays ŌåÆ 'string[]',
 *        if all match ISO date pattern ŌåÆ 'date',
 *        else ŌåÆ 'string'
 */
export function inferFieldType(values: unknown[]): FrontmatterField['type']

/**
 * Extract a specific field as time-series data points.
 * Returns { date (ms timestamp), value (number or null) } for each entry.
 * Non-numeric fields return null values.
 */
export function getFieldTimeSeries(
    entries: JournalEntry[],
    fieldKey: string
): MetricDataPoint[]
```

**`src/services/JournalIndexService.ts`** (~300 lines)

The core indexing engine. This service has an Obsidian API dependency (Vault, MetadataCache, TFile, TFolder):
```typescript
import { App, TFile, TFolder, normalizePath, Notice } from 'obsidian';
import type HindsightPlugin from '../../main';

// Debounce delay for file change events (ms)
const DEBOUNCE_MS = 400;
// Batch size for pass 2 background content parsing
const PARSE_BATCH_SIZE = 50;

export class JournalIndexService {
    private app: App;
    private plugin: HindsightPlugin;
    private journalFolder: string; // normalizePath'd
    private debounceTimers: Map<string, ReturnType<typeof setTimeout>>;

    constructor(app: App, plugin: HindsightPlugin) {
        this.journalFolder = normalizePath(plugin.settings.journalFolder);
        ...
    }

    /**
     * Two-pass initialization. Delegates to runPass1() and runPass2().
     * Called once on plugin load via workspace.onLayoutReady().
     */
    async initialize(): Promise<void> {
        await this.runPass1();
        await this.runPass2();
    }

    /**
     * PASS 1 (instant, no file I/O):
     *   - Validates journalFolder by calling getFolderByPath().
     *     If the folder doesn't exist, shows a Notice and returns early.
     *     This implicitly blocks path traversal (../../ won't resolve).
     *   - Recursively scan for .md files matching filename pattern
     *   - For each candidate: metadataCache.getFileCache(file) for frontmatter
     *   - Extract date from frontmatter `date` field (authoritative), fall back to filename
     *   - Create JournalEntry with frontmatter populated, sections/wordCount/imagePaths empty
     *   - Set fullyIndexed = false
     *   - Uses store.setEntries() (bulk) ŌĆö sorts sortedDates once
     *   - Calls detectFields() ONCE after all entries are populated
     *   - Updates store.indexingProgress to { phase: 1, processed: N, total: N }
     */
    private async runPass1(): Promise<void>

    /**
     * PASS 2 (background, batched):
     *   - Process files in chunks of PARSE_BATCH_SIZE
     *   - For each file: vault.cachedRead() ŌåÆ parse sections, word count, image paths
     *   - Yield to main thread between batches via setTimeout(0)
     *   - Uses store.upsertEntries() (bulk) per batch ŌĆö one sort per batch, not per entry
     *   - Set fullyIndexed = true per entry
     *   - Compute qualityScore per entry based on detected fields vs filled fields
     *   - Updates store.indexingProgress as batches complete
     *   - Calls detectFields() ONE MORE TIME after all batches finish
     *     (for accurate coverage/ranges with full data)
     */
    private async runPass2(): Promise<void>

    /**
     * Recursively scan a folder for .md files matching the journal filename pattern.
     * Returns TFile references for all matching files.
     */
    private scanFolder(folder: TFolder): TFile[]

    /**
     * Parse frontmatter-only entry (pass 1).
     * Uses metadataCache.getFileCache() ŌĆö zero file I/O.
     * Date is sourced from frontmatter `date` field; falls back to filename regex.
     */
    parseEntryFrontmatterOnly(file: TFile): JournalEntry | null

    /**
     * Parse full content for an entry (pass 2).
     * Uses vault.cachedRead() for content.
     * Uses SectionParserService for sections, word count, and images.
     * Updates the existing entry in place.
     */
    async parseEntryContent(file: TFile, entry: JournalEntry): Promise<void>

    /**
     * Re-index with a new journal folder.
     * Called when the user changes the folder in settings (via onBlur).
     * Clears the store, updates this.journalFolder, and re-runs both passes.
     */
    async reconfigure(newFolder: string): Promise<void> {
        this.journalFolder = normalizePath(newFolder);
        useJournalStore.getState().clear();
        await this.initialize();
    }

    /**
     * Register file watchers for create/delete/rename events AND metadata changes.
     * Uses plugin.registerEvent() for automatic cleanup on unload.
     *
     * EVENT ARCHITECTURE:
     *   - metadataCache.on('changed', (file, data, cache) => ...)
     *     ŌåÆ Used for frontmatter updates. This fires AFTER the cache has been
     *       updated, avoiding the race condition of vault.on('modify') + getFileCache().
     *     ŌåÆ Debounced by DEBOUNCE_MS to avoid re-parsing on every keystroke.
     *     ŌåÆ Checks file.stat.mtime against stored entry.mtime to skip no-ops.
     *   - vault.on('create', callback)
     *     ŌåÆ Parses if it matches filename pattern, adds to store.
     *   - vault.on('delete', callback)
     *     ŌåÆ Removes from store.
     *   - vault.on('rename', (file, oldPath) => ...)
     *     ŌåÆ Removes old path, adds new if it matches pattern.
     *
     * All handlers check file instanceof TFile and file.path starts with journalFolder.
     */
    registerFileWatchers(): void

    /** Clean up debounce timers and any resources (called from plugin.onunload()) */
    destroy(): void
}
```

**Key Obsidian API usage:**
- `app.vault.getFolderByPath(normalizePath(folderPath))` to get the root folder ŌĆö returns null if folder doesn't exist (implicit path traversal guard)
- `normalizePath()` on the journal folder setting in the constructor
- Iterate `folder.children`, recurse into `TFolder` instances, collect `TFile` instances
- `app.metadataCache.getFileCache(file)?.frontmatter` for frontmatter (fast, cached)
- `app.vault.cachedRead(file)` for full content (pass 2 only, batched in background)
- `plugin.registerEvent(app.metadataCache.on('changed', callback))` for metadata watching (NOT `vault.on('modify')`)
- `plugin.registerEvent(app.vault.on('create', callback))` for new files
- `plugin.registerEvent(app.vault.on('delete', callback))` for deletions
- `plugin.registerEvent(app.vault.on('rename', callback))` for renames
- Check `file instanceof TFile` and `file.path.startsWith(this.journalFolder)` before processing
- `normalizePath()` on all constructed paths
- Debounce modify handlers with `setTimeout` (clear previous timer per file path)

**`src/store/journalStore.ts`** (~120 lines)
```typescript
import { create } from 'zustand';
import type { JournalEntry, FrontmatterField, DateRange } from '../types';
import { formatDateISO } from '../utils/dateUtils';

interface IndexingProgress {
    /** Current indexing phase (1 = frontmatter only, 2 = full content) */
    phase: 1 | 2;
    /** Number of files processed in current phase */
    processed: number;
    /** Total files to process in current phase */
    total: number;
}

interface JournalState {
    /** All indexed entries, keyed by vault-relative file path */
    entries: Map<string, JournalEntry>;
    /** Date-keyed index for O(1) echo lookups. Key: "MM-DD", Value: entries for that day across all years */
    dateIndex: Map<string, JournalEntry[]>;
    /** Dates with entries, sorted ascending (for quick range lookups) */
    sortedDates: Date[];
    /** Cached sorted entries array (newest first). Invalidated on entry changes. */
    cachedSortedEntries: JournalEntry[] | null;
    /** Detected frontmatter fields across all entries */
    detectedFields: FrontmatterField[];
    /** Whether the initial scan is in progress */
    loading: boolean;
    /** Error message if scan failed */
    error: string | null;
    /** Indexing progress for pass 1/2 ŌĆö used for progress bar UI */
    indexingProgress: IndexingProgress | null;
}

interface JournalActions {
    /** Bulk set all entries (pass 1). Builds dateIndex and sortedDates in one pass. */
    setEntries(entries: JournalEntry[]): void;
    /** Update a single entry. Uses binary insertion for sortedDates. Invalidates cache. */
    upsertEntry(entry: JournalEntry): void;
    /** Bulk update multiple entries (pass 2 batches). Sorts once at end. Invalidates cache. */
    upsertEntries(entries: JournalEntry[]): void;
    /** Remove an entry by file path. Invalidates cache. */
    removeEntry(filePath: string): void;
    /** Clear all entries and indexes (used by reconfigure). */
    clear(): void;
    setDetectedFields(fields: FrontmatterField[]): void;
    setLoading(loading: boolean): void;
    setError(error: string | null): void;
    setIndexingProgress(progress: IndexingProgress | null): void;

    /** Get entries within a date range (inclusive) */
    getEntriesInRange(range: DateRange): JournalEntry[];
    /** Get entry for a specific date (first match) */
    getEntryByDate(date: Date): JournalEntry | undefined;
    /**
     * Get all entries as a sorted array (newest first).
     * Returns a cached array ŌĆö only rebuilds when entries actually change.
     * Components should use this instead of spreading entries.values().
     */
    getAllEntriesSorted(): JournalEntry[];
    /**
     * Get entries for a specific month-day across all years (for echoes).
     * O(1) lookup via dateIndex. Key format: "MM-DD".
     */
    getEntriesByMonthDay(monthDay: string): JournalEntry[];
}

export const useJournalStore = create<JournalState & JournalActions>((set, get) => ({
    // ... implementation
    // Note: upsertEntry uses binary insertion into sortedDates
    // to avoid O(n log n) full re-sort on every entry update.
    // upsertEntries batches multiple updates and sorts once.
}));
```

> **Performance notes:**
> - `cachedSortedEntries` is a stable array reference. It's only set to `null` (invalidated) when entries change. `getAllEntriesSorted()` rebuilds it lazily on next call. This means hooks like `useEchoes` don't rebuild arrays on every unrelated store change.
> - `dateIndex` maps `"MM-DD"` strings to entry arrays, enabling O(1) echo lookups instead of O(n) scans.
> - `upsertEntries()` is used by pass 2 batches to avoid 50 individual sorts per batch.
> - `uiStore` remains a single store for now (sidebar tabs, main tabs, calendar state, sort/filter). If re-render issues emerge, consider splitting into `calendarStore` and `indexStore`.

**`src/store/settingsStore.ts`** (~30 lines)

Reactive mirror of plugin settings for React components:
```typescript
import { create } from 'zustand';
import type { HindsightSettings } from '../types';
import { DEFAULT_SETTINGS } from '../types';

interface SettingsState {
    settings: HindsightSettings;
    setSettings(settings: HindsightSettings): void;
}

export const useSettingsStore = create<SettingsState>((set) => ({
    settings: DEFAULT_SETTINGS,
    setSettings: (settings) => set({ settings }),
}));
```

### main.ts Updates

```typescript
// Add to onload():
import { JournalIndexService } from './src/services/JournalIndexService';
import { useSettingsStore } from './src/store/settingsStore';

// In onload(), after loadSettings():
useSettingsStore.getState().setSettings(this.settings);

this.journalIndex = new JournalIndexService(this.app, this);
this.app.workspace.onLayoutReady(async () => {
    await this.journalIndex.initialize();
    this.journalIndex.registerFileWatchers();
});

// Temporary debug command (remove after Phase 1 verification):
this.addCommand({
    id: 'debug-index',
    name: 'Debug: log journal index',
    callback: () => {
        const { entries, detectedFields } = useJournalStore.getState();
        console.debug(`Hindsight index: ${entries.size} entries`);
        console.debug('Detected fields:', detectedFields);
        if (entries.size > 0) {
            const sample = entries.values().next().value;
            console.debug('Sample entry:', sample);
        }
    },
});

// In onunload():
this.journalIndex?.destroy();
```

9. Delete a daily note ŌåÆ it's removed from the index

**`test/utils/fileNameParser.test.ts`** (~80 lines)

```
Tests:
- Valid filenames: "2026-03-05, Thursday.md" ŌåÆ correct date + dayOfWeek
- Various days of week: Monday through Sunday
- Different years/months
- Edge dates: Jan 1, Dec 31, Feb 29 (leap year), Feb 28
- Invalid filenames: returns null
  - Missing day of week: "2026-03-05.md"
  - Wrong extension: "2026-03-05, Thursday.txt"
  - Bad date: "2026-02-31, Monday.md" (Feb 31 doesn't exist)
  - No comma: "2026-03-05 Thursday.md"
  - Empty string, random text
  - Just the date with no file extension
```

## Phase 2: Sidebar View ŌĆö Today + Echoes Ō£ģ COMPLETE

**Goal:** Ship the first visible UI. A sidebar view showing today's entry status and "on this day" echoes from past years. Uses the React-in-ItemView pattern from Quest Board.

### Files to Create

**`src/services/EchoesService.ts`** (~60 lines)

Pure functions ŌĆö takes entries array or dateIndex, returns filtered results:
```typescript
import type { JournalEntry } from '../types';
import { isSameDay, isSameWeek, formatDateISO } from '../utils/dateUtils';

/**
 * Find entries from the same date in previous years.
 * Uses the store's dateIndex for O(1) lookup by "MM-DD" key.
 * Filters out entries from the current year.
 */
export function getOnThisDay(
    targetDate: Date,
    dateIndex: Map<string, JournalEntry[]>
): JournalEntry[]

/**
 * Find entries from the same ISO week in previous years.
 * Returns entries grouped by year.
 */
export function getThisWeekLastYear(
    targetDate: Date,
    entries: JournalEntry[]
): JournalEntry[]
```

**`src/services/PulseService.ts`** (~60 lines, starter ŌĆö expanded in Phase 6)

```typescript
/**
 * Calculate the current writing streak (consecutive days with entries ending today).
 * Returns 0 if no entry today.
 */
export function getCurrentStreak(entries: JournalEntry[]): number

/**
```

**`src/hooks/useEchoes.ts`** (~30 lines)
```typescript
export function useEchoes() {
    // Use the dateIndex for O(1) echo lookups
    const dateIndex = useJournalStore(state => state.dateIndex);
    const entries = useJournalStore(state => state.getAllEntriesSorted());
    const today = useToday(); // custom hook ŌĆö see below

    const monthDay = `${String(today.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0')}-${String(today.getDate()).padStart(2, '0')}`;

    return useMemo(() => ({
        onThisDay: getOnThisDay(today, dateIndex),
        thisWeekLastYear: getThisWeekLastYear(today, entries),
    }), [monthDay, dateIndex, entries]);
}
```

**`src/hooks/useToday.ts`** (~20 lines)
```typescript
/**
 * Returns today's date as a stable reference.
 * Automatically refreshes at midnight so the sidebar never shows stale data
 * if left open overnight.
 */
export function useToday(): Date {
    const [today, setToday] = useState(() => startOfDay(new Date()));

    useEffect(() => {
        const check = setInterval(() => {
            const now = startOfDay(new Date());
            if (formatDateISO(now) !== formatDateISO(today)) {
                setToday(now);
            }
        }, 60_000); // check every 60 seconds
        return () => clearInterval(check);
    }, [today]);

    return today;
}
```

**`src/hooks/useSettings.ts`** (~10 lines)
```typescript
export function useSettings() {
    return useSettingsStore(state => state.settings);
}
```

**`src/views/HindsightSidebarView.tsx`** (~50 lines)

Follow the Quest Board ItemView pattern exactly:
```typescript
import { ItemView, WorkspaceLeaf } from 'obsidian';
import { createRoot, Root } from 'react-dom/client';
import { HINDSIGHT_SIDEBAR_VIEW_TYPE } from '../constants';
import { SidebarApp } from '../components/SidebarApp';
import type HindsightPlugin from '../../main';

export class HindsightSidebarView extends ItemView {
    private root: Root | null = null;
    private plugin: HindsightPlugin;

    constructor(leaf: WorkspaceLeaf, plugin: HindsightPlugin) {
        super(leaf);
        this.plugin = plugin;
    }

    getViewType(): string { return HINDSIGHT_SIDEBAR_VIEW_TYPE; }
    getDisplayText(): string { return 'Hindsight'; }
    getIcon(): string { return 'history'; }

    async onOpen(): Promise<void> {
        const container = this.containerEl.children[1];
        container.empty();
        container.addClass('hindsight-sidebar-container');
        this.root = createRoot(container as HTMLElement);
        this.root.render(
            <ErrorBoundary fallback="Hindsight sidebar encountered an error.">
                <SidebarApp plugin={this.plugin} app={this.app} />
            </ErrorBoundary>
        );
    }

    async onClose(): Promise<void> {
        if (this.root) {
            this.root.unmount();
            this.root = null;
        }
    }
}
```

> **ErrorBoundary:** Create `src/components/shared/ErrorBoundary.tsx` ŌĆö a React class component
> that catches render errors and shows a fallback UI with a "Reload" button (calls
> `this.setState({ hasError: false })` to re-mount children). This prevents a single
> component crash from blanking the entire view.
> CSS class: `hindsight-error-boundary`

**`src/components/SidebarApp.tsx`** (~40 lines)
Root sidebar component with tab switching:
- Two tabs: "Today" and "Echoes"
- Uses `TabSwitcher` component
- Renders `TodayStatus` or `EchoesPanel` based on active tab
- Props: `plugin: HindsightPlugin`, `app: App`

**`src/components/shared/TabSwitcher.tsx`** (~30 lines)
Reusable tab bar:
- Props: `tabs: { id: string, label: string }[]`, `activeTab: string`, `onTabChange: (id: string) => void`
- Renders a row of buttons with `hindsight-tab` and `hindsight-tab-active` classes
- 44px minimum touch targets for mobile

**`src/components/sidebar/TodayStatus.tsx`** (~70 lines)
- Shows whether today's entry exists (green check or gray indicator)
- If it exists: shows filled fields count / total detected fields, word count
- Shows current writing streak from `PulseService.getCurrentStreak()`
- **Relative time indicator:** "Last entry: 2 hours ago" or "Last entry: yesterday" ŌĆö updates every 60 seconds via the `useToday()` hook's interval
- "Open today's note" button ŌĆö uses `app.workspace.openLinkText(filePath, '')` to navigate
- If no entry: shows "No entry yet today" with friendly empty state

**`src/components/echoes/EchoesPanel.tsx`** (~50 lines)

### main.ts Updates
```typescript
// Add to imports:
import { HindsightSidebarView } from './src/views/HindsightSidebarView';
import { HINDSIGHT_SIDEBAR_VIEW_TYPE } from './src/constants';

// In onload(), after journal index setup:
this.registerView(
    HINDSIGHT_SIDEBAR_VIEW_TYPE,
    (leaf) => new HindsightSidebarView(leaf, this)
);

this.addCommand({
    id: 'open-sidebar',
    name: 'Open sidebar',
    callback: () => this.activateSidebarView(),
});

// Auto-open sidebar if enabled:
if (this.settings.enableSidebar) {
    this.app.workspace.onLayoutReady(() => this.activateSidebarView());
}

// Helper method on the plugin class:
async activateSidebarView(): Promise<void> {
    const leaves = this.app.workspace.getLeavesOfType(HINDSIGHT_SIDEBAR_VIEW_TYPE);
    if (leaves.length === 0) {
        const leaf = this.app.workspace.getLeftLeaf(false);
        if (leaf) {
            await leaf.setViewState({ type: HINDSIGHT_SIDEBAR_VIEW_TYPE });
        }
    } else {
        this.app.workspace.revealLeaf(leaves[0]);
    }
}
```

Same ItemView pattern as sidebar but full-page:
```typescript
import { ItemView, WorkspaceLeaf } from 'obsidian';
import { createRoot, Root } from 'react-dom/client';
import { HINDSIGHT_MAIN_VIEW_TYPE } from '../constants';
import { MainApp } from '../components/MainApp';
import type HindsightPlugin from '../../main';

export class HindsightMainView extends ItemView {
    private root: Root | null = null;
    private plugin: HindsightPlugin;

    constructor(leaf: WorkspaceLeaf, plugin: HindsightPlugin) {
        super(leaf);
        this.plugin = plugin;
    }

    getViewType(): string { return HINDSIGHT_MAIN_VIEW_TYPE; }
    getDisplayText(): string { return 'Hindsight'; }
    getIcon(): string { return 'book-open'; }

    async onOpen(): Promise<void> {
        const container = this.containerEl.children[1];
        container.empty();
        container.addClass('hindsight-main-container');
        this.root = createRoot(container as HTMLElement);
        this.root.render(
            <ErrorBoundary fallback="Hindsight encountered an error.">
                <MainApp plugin={this.plugin} app={this.app} />
            </ErrorBoundary>
        );
    }

    async onClose(): Promise<void> {
        if (this.root) {
            this.root.unmount();
            this.root = null;
        }
    }
}
```

**`src/utils/statsUtils.ts`** (~50 lines)
```typescript
/**
 * Map a numeric value to a color on a red-yellow-green gradient.
 * Returns a CSS color string.
 * Uses HSL interpolation: 0 (red, hsl 0) ŌåÆ 60 (yellow) ŌåÆ 120 (green)
 * Null values return a neutral color (--background-modifier-border).
 */
export function mapValueToColor(
    value: number | null,
    min: number,
    max: number
): string

/**
 * Map a boolean value to a color.
 * true ŌåÆ green (--text-success), false/null ŌåÆ red (--text-error)
 */
export function mapBooleanToColor(value: boolean | null): string
```

## Phase 4: Timeline + Journal Index (~1-2 sessions) Ō£ģ COMPLETE

**Goal:** Complete the three core navigation modes. Timeline is a scrollable card feed. Index is a sortable/filterable data table. Both read from the same journal store.

### Files to Create

**`src/components/timeline/TimelineList.tsx`** (~70 lines)

Paginated entry card list:
- Props: `app: App` (for opening notes on click)
- Reads from `useJournalStore` ŌåÆ `getAllEntriesSorted()` (stable cached reference)
- Shows `ENTRIES_PER_PAGE = 50` entries per page with "Load more" button
- Sort toggle: newest first (default) or oldest first
- Each entry rendered as `EntryCard`
- Uses `VirtualList` from `shared/` for scroll performance (see below)

**`src/components/shared/VirtualList.tsx`** (~80 lines)

Lightweight virtual scroll component (no external dependency):
- Props: `items: T[]`, `renderItem: (item: T, index: number) => ReactNode`, `estimatedItemHeight: number`, `overscan?: number` (default 10)
- Measures the scroll container height and current scroll position
- Computes the visible window: `startIndex = Math.floor(scrollTop / estimatedItemHeight) - overscan`, `endIndex = startIndex + visibleCount + 2 * overscan`
- Renders a spacer div above (height = startIndex * estimatedItemHeight) and below for the remaining items
- Only renders items within the visible window + buffer
- Uses `useRef` for the scroll container and `useEffect` with a scroll event listener
- CSS class: `hindsight-virtual-list` (overflow-y: auto, flex: 1)

**`src/components/timeline/EntryCard.tsx`** (~60 lines)

Entry summary card:
- Props: `entry: JournalEntry`, `detectedFields: FrontmatterField[]`, `onClick: () => void`
- Shows:
  - Date + day of week (e.g., "March 5, 2026 ŌĆö Thursday")
  - Mood and energy badges (if those fields exist ŌĆö check `detectedFields`)
  - **Entry quality score** as a small progress ring or percentage badge
  - Word count badge
  - Tags (from frontmatter `tags` field, if present)
  - Excerpt: Uses `stripMarkdown()` on section content first, THEN truncates to ~150 chars. Source: `entry.sections['What Actually Happened']`, falls back to first non-empty section value. **Never slice raw markdown** ŌĆö always clean to plain text first.
  - Image count badge (e.g., "2 images") if `entry.imagePaths.length > 0`
- Click handler opens the note
- CSS class: `hindsight-entry-card`

**`src/components/index-table/JournalIndex.tsx`** (~100 lines)

Sortable data table:
- Props: `app: App`
- Reads from journal store (all entries) + detected fields
- Columns:
  - **Date** ŌĆö formatted date string, sortable
  - **Day** ŌĆö day of week
  - **Word count** ŌĆö number, sortable
  - **Dynamic columns** ŌĆö one per detected numeric/boolean field (mood, energy, etc.), sortable
  - **Tags** ŌĆö comma-separated tag list
- Click row ŌåÆ opens the note
- Sort state from `uiStore.indexSort`
- Click column header to toggle sort (asc/desc)
- Uses a plain HTML `<table>` ŌĆö no library. Obsidian's base table styles apply, with `hindsight-` prefixed class overrides.

**`src/components/index-table/IndexFilters.tsx`** (~70 lines)

Search and filter bar above the table:
- **Text search input** ŌĆö filters entries by searching `entry.sections` values (case insensitive). For full-text search across all content, lazy-loads via `vault.cachedRead()` on demand (since `rawContent` is not stored in the entry). **Debounced at 250ms** to avoid filtering on every keystroke with 700+ entries.
- **Date range filter** ŌĆö two date inputs (from/to), filters entries within range
- **Field filters** ŌĆö for each numeric detected field, optional min/max inputs. E.g., "Mood Ōēź 7"
- **Clear all button** ŌĆö resets all filters
- Filter state stored in `uiStore.indexFilters`
- Filters are applied in the component (derived state from store entries + filter config)

**`src/store/uiStore.ts`** ŌĆö Updated to add:
```typescript
// Index sort
indexSort: { field: string; direction: 'asc' | 'desc' };
setIndexSort(field: string): void;  // Toggles direction if same field, sets asc if new field

// Index filters
indexFilters: {
    search: string;
    dateRange: DateRange | null;
    fieldFilters: Array<{ field: string; operator: '>=' | '<=' | '='; value: number }>;
};
setSearchFilter(search: string): void;
setDateRangeFilter(range: DateRange | null): void;
addFieldFilter(field: string, operator: string, value: number): void;
removeFieldFilter(index: number): void;
clearAllFilters(): void;
```

**`src/styles/timeline.css`**

   **Type safety:** Use a discriminated union type for `LensFilterRow` rather than optional fields: `type LensFilterRow = { type: "field"; fieldKey: string; operator: ">=" | "<=" | "=" | "!="; value: string | number } | { type: "dateRange"; startDate: string; endDate: string } | { type: "tag"; tag: string } | ...`.
